# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
The brain as a radio
Transmitter, creating reality
Using signals of energy it perceives through the senses ^v4fz5CER

As well as energy manifesting as physical
Things in our vision, they can also be tuned into
As thoughts and visions in the mental experience too ^NUIEjtjN
